\mbox{\Hypertarget{classbasic__json_a5ea129b0e5c10074c3dce7e39041696b}\label{classbasic__json_a5ea129b0e5c10074c3dce7e39041696b}} 
\index{basic\_json@{basic\_json}!assert\_invariant@{assert\_invariant}}
\index{assert\_invariant@{assert\_invariant}!basic\_json@{basic\_json}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{assert\_invariant()}{assert\_invariant()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void basic\+\_\+json\+::assert\+\_\+invariant (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{check\+\_\+parents = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{mic__base_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [private]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



checks the class invariants 

This function asserts the class invariants. It needs to be called at the end of every constructor to make sure that created objects respect the invariant. Furthermore, it has to be called each time the type of a J\+S\+ON value is changed, because the invariant expresses a relationship between {\itshape m\+\_\+type} and {\itshape m\+\_\+value}.

Furthermore, the parent relation is checked for arrays and objects\+: If {\itshape check\+\_\+parents} true and the value is an array or object, then the container\textquotesingle{}s elements must have the current value as parent.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em check\+\_\+parents} & whether the parent relation should be checked. The value is true by default and should only be set to false during destruction of objects when the invariant does not need to hold. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{classbasic__json_a375f9138e76cef595fded384a8fcdc4c}\label{classbasic__json_a375f9138e76cef595fded384a8fcdc4c}}

get a (pointer) value (explicit) 

Performs explicit type conversion between the J\+S\+ON value and a compatible value if required.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If the requested type is a pointer to the internally stored J\+S\+ON value that pointer is returned. No copies are made.
\item If the requested type is the current \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}}, or a different \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}} convertible from the current \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}}.
\item Otherwise the value is converted by calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ac06cbf6ad38062e2b7fcb996e9ace17b}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$}} {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a6b60b3f3a22e35323af3ecbb1d7e2464}{from\+\_\+json()}}} method.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type\+CV} & the provided value type \\
\hline
{\em Value\+Type} & the returned value type\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
copy of the J\+S\+ON value, converted to 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type} & if necessary\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em what} & \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ac06cbf6ad38062e2b7fcb996e9ace17b}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$}} {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a6b60b3f3a22e35323af3ecbb1d7e2464}{from\+\_\+json()}}} method throws if conversion is required\\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

\end{DoxySince}

auto basic\+\_\+json\+::get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) -\/$>$ decltype(std\+::declval$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ab07a1a9d14a18782efb99a9700d03f23}{basic\+\_\+json\+\_\+t}}\&$>$().template \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ac290e2691604a7c9f1511f15f56953f7}{get\+\_\+ptr}}$<$Pointer\+Type$>$())

get a pointer value (explicit) 

Explicit pointer access to the internally stored J\+S\+ON value. No copies are made.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The pointer becomes invalid if the underlying J\+S\+ON object changes.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Pointer\+Type} & pointer type; must be a pointer to \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a2633e83ba602f57fe99ce2443765e523}{array\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a5196defd1adc1835fc9ef0e53fa04ef8}{object\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a413818018f56cc0d49824c51bc5a2986}{string\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_aa0c69a44d0bc75ccefbb819b073c35f1}{boolean\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a39479d4834fe2ae2971809183a2a1fac}{number\+\_\+integer\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_af1142f3b7e5999175c958821fac46514}{number\+\_\+unsigned\+\_\+t}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_aa0845824a65b759ba5cd8b963c159a81}{number\+\_\+float\+\_\+t}}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
pointer to the internally stored J\+S\+ON value if the requested pointer type {\itshape Pointer\+Type} fits to the J\+S\+ON value; {\ttfamily nullptr} otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
@complexity Constant.

@liveexample\{The example below shows how pointers to internal values of a J\+S\+ON value can be requested. Note that no type conversions are made and a {\ttfamily nullptr} is returned if the value and the requested pointer type does not match.,get\+\_\+\+\_\+\+Pointer\+Type\}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
see \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ac290e2691604a7c9f1511f15f56953f7}{get\+\_\+ptr()}} for explicit pointer-\/member access
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

get a value (explicit) 

Explicit type conversion between the J\+S\+ON value and a compatible value which is \href{https://en.cppreference.com/w/cpp/named_req/CopyConstructible}{\texttt{ Copy\+Constructible}} and \href{https://en.cppreference.com/w/cpp/named_req/DefaultConstructible}{\texttt{ Default\+Constructible}}. The value is converted by calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ac06cbf6ad38062e2b7fcb996e9ace17b}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$}} {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a6b60b3f3a22e35323af3ecbb1d7e2464}{from\+\_\+json()}}} method.

The function is equivalent to executing 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{ValueType ret;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_ac8fc7fc4703cbd8edd7bb43a94adf92b}{JSONSerializer<ValueType>::from\_json}}(*\textcolor{keyword}{this}, ret);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ret;}
\end{DoxyCode}


This overloads is chosen if\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\itshape Value\+Type} is not \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}},
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ac06cbf6ad38062e2b7fcb996e9ace17b}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$}} has a {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a6b60b3f3a22e35323af3ecbb1d7e2464}{from\+\_\+json()}}} method of the form {\ttfamily void from\+\_\+json(const basic\+\_\+json\&, Value\+Type\&)}, and
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ac06cbf6ad38062e2b7fcb996e9ace17b}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$}} does not have a {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a6b60b3f3a22e35323af3ecbb1d7e2464}{from\+\_\+json()}}} method of the form {\ttfamily Value\+Type from\+\_\+json(const basic\+\_\+json\&)}
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type} & the returned value type\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
copy of the J\+S\+ON value, converted to {\itshape Value\+Type} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em what} & \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ac06cbf6ad38062e2b7fcb996e9ace17b}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$}} {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a6b60b3f3a22e35323af3ecbb1d7e2464}{from\+\_\+json()}}} method throws\\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}
@liveexample\{The example below shows several conversions from J\+S\+ON values to other types. There a few things to note\+: (1) Floating-\/point numbers can be converted to integers\textbackslash{}, (2) A J\+S\+ON array can be converted to a standard {\ttfamily std\+::vector$<$short$>$}\textbackslash{}, (3) A J\+S\+ON object can be converted to C++ associative containers such as {\ttfamily std\+::unordered\+\_\+map$<$std\+::string\textbackslash{}, json$>$}.,get\+\_\+\+\_\+\+Value\+Type\+\_\+const\}

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 2.\+1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

get a value (explicit); special case 

Explicit type conversion between the J\+S\+ON value and a compatible value which is {\bfseries{not}} \href{https://en.cppreference.com/w/cpp/named_req/CopyConstructible}{\texttt{ Copy\+Constructible}} and {\bfseries{not}} \href{https://en.cppreference.com/w/cpp/named_req/DefaultConstructible}{\texttt{ Default\+Constructible}}. The value is converted by calling the \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ac06cbf6ad38062e2b7fcb996e9ace17b}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$}} {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a6b60b3f3a22e35323af3ecbb1d7e2464}{from\+\_\+json()}}} method.

The function is equivalent to executing 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_ac8fc7fc4703cbd8edd7bb43a94adf92b}{JSONSerializer<ValueType>::from\_json}}(*\textcolor{keyword}{this});}
\end{DoxyCode}


This overloads is chosen if\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\itshape Value\+Type} is not \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}} and
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ac06cbf6ad38062e2b7fcb996e9ace17b}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$}} has a {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a6b60b3f3a22e35323af3ecbb1d7e2464}{from\+\_\+json()}}} method of the form {\ttfamily Value\+Type from\+\_\+json(const basic\+\_\+json\&)}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ac06cbf6ad38062e2b7fcb996e9ace17b}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$}} has both overloads of {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a6b60b3f3a22e35323af3ecbb1d7e2464}{from\+\_\+json()}}}, this one is chosen.
\end{DoxyNote}

\end{DoxyWarning}

{\em Pointer\+Type} & pointer type; must be a pointer to \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a2633e83ba602f57fe99ce2443765e523}{array\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a5196defd1adc1835fc9ef0e53fa04ef8}{object\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a413818018f56cc0d49824c51bc5a2986}{string\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_aa0c69a44d0bc75ccefbb819b073c35f1}{boolean\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a39479d4834fe2ae2971809183a2a1fac}{number\+\_\+integer\+\_\+t}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_af1142f3b7e5999175c958821fac46514}{number\+\_\+unsigned\+\_\+t}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_aa0845824a65b759ba5cd8b963c159a81}{number\+\_\+float\+\_\+t}}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
pointer to the internally stored J\+S\+ON value if the requested pointer type {\itshape Pointer\+Type} fits to the J\+S\+ON value; {\ttfamily nullptr} otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
@complexity Constant.

@liveexample\{The example below shows how pointers to internal values of a J\+S\+ON value can be requested. Note that no type conversions are made and a {\ttfamily nullptr} is returned if the value and the requested pointer type does not match.,get\+\_\+\+\_\+\+Pointer\+Type\}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Value\+Type , typename std\+::enable\+\_\+if$<$ detail\+::conjunction$<$ detail\+::negation$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+pointer$<$ Value\+Type $>$$>$, detail\+::negation$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Value\+Type, std\+::nullptr\+\_\+t $>$$>$, detail\+::negation$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Value\+Type, detail\+::json\+\_\+ref$<$ basic\+\_\+json $>$$>$$>$, detail\+::negation$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Value\+Type, typename string\+\_\+t\+::value\+\_\+type $>$$>$, detail\+::negation$<$ detail\+::is\+\_\+basic\+\_\+json$<$ Value\+Type $>$$>$, detail\+::negation$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Value\+Type, std\+::initializer\+\_\+list$<$ typename string\+\_\+t\+::value\+\_\+type $>$$>$$>$, detail\+::is\+\_\+detected\+\_\+lazy$<$ detail\+::get\+\_\+template\+\_\+function, const basic\+\_\+json\+\_\+t \&, Value\+Type $>$ $>$\+::value, int $>$\+::type  = 0$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{json_8hpp_aefed8cf27cadeea45f12c6f3db3ce774}{J\+S\+O\+N\+\_\+\+E\+X\+P\+L\+I\+C\+IT}} basic\+\_\+json\+::operator Value\+Type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



get a value (implicit) 

Implicit type conversion between the J\+S\+ON value and a compatible value. The call is realized by calling \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_aa78293304f1532d1715ef24e21fed598}{get() const}}.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type} & non-\/pointer type compatible to the J\+S\+ON value, for instance {\ttfamily int} for J\+S\+ON integer numbers, {\ttfamily bool} for J\+S\+ON booleans, or {\ttfamily std\+::vector} types for J\+S\+ON arrays. The character type of \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a413818018f56cc0d49824c51bc5a2986}{string\+\_\+t}} as well as an initializer list of this type is excluded to avoid ambiguities as these types implicitly convert to {\ttfamily std\+::string}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
copy of the J\+S\+ON value, converted to type {\itshape Value\+Type} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em type\+\_\+error.\+302} & in case passed type {\itshape Value\+Type} is incompatible to the J\+S\+ON value type (e.\+g., the J\+S\+ON value is of type boolean, but a string is requested); see example below\\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}
@complexity Linear in the size of the J\+S\+ON value.

@liveexample\{The example below shows several conversions from J\+S\+ON values to other types. There a few things to note\+: (1) Floating-\/point numbers can be converted to integers\textbackslash{}, (2) A J\+S\+ON array can be converted to a standard {\ttfamily std\+::vector$<$short$>$}\textbackslash{}, (3) A J\+S\+ON object can be converted to C++ associative containers such as {\ttfamily std\+::unordered\+\_\+map$<$std\+::string\textbackslash{}, json$>$}.,operator\+\_\+\+\_\+\+Value\+Type\}

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 1.\+0.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}
